E si la humiditat es en le propri pannicol, lahoras le apostema es redon am partida del huou e per aysso hom estima que es autre huou.
If the moisture is in the membrane itself, the swelling is round with part of the testicle, and thus it is thought to be another testicle.

E si la humiditat es entre la codena dels genetius e·l ciphac blanc, lahoras catz dejos le centiment.
If the moisture is between the genital covering and the white sac, it falls below the perception.

E cum tu vols la cognicio de la color de la humiditat, lahoras tu esproa la color de la humiditat en le apostema am entromes cayrat del qual la forma es precedida; e segon aquo que es eyssit en le vestigi del entromes, jutga de aquo que es dedintz lu.
When you want to determine the color of the moisture, you test the color of the moisture in the swelling with a square probe; and based on what comes out in the mark from the probe, you judge what is inside.

Donc quan nos vinem a la curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que comandem al malaute que sia fleubotomat si aquo es a tu possibla, e vezes le cos de lu ple.
When we come to treating it with surgery, we should instruct the patient to be bled if possible, and cleanse his body fully.

E aprop sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos sobre alcuna causa un pauc auta, e pausa dejos lu motz draps.
Then let him lie on his back on a slightly elevated surface, and place many cloths under him.

E aprop setz tu sobre la part sinistra de lu, e comanda al ministra que segua a la dextra de lu, le qual extenda la sua vergua a hun de dos latz a la codena dels genetius e a la partida del mirac del ventre.
Sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant to be on his right side, who will extend his penis to one of two sides to the covering of the genitals and the lower part of the abdomen.

E aprop pren spatum lat e scindeys la codena dels genetius del mieg loc per la longitut entro prop le pentenilh.
Then take a broad knife and cut the genital covering in the middle along its length down to near the pubic bone.

E sia fayta la seccio segon rectetut engualment distant de la linha que deveseys la pel dels genetius, entro que pervengua al ciphac blanc comprehendent.
The incision should be made straight and equally distant from the line dividing the skin of the genitals, until it reaches the white sac.

E excorja aquel, e observa, e guarda te per aysso que tu no inscidas aquel; e la tua excoriacio am la qual aquel excorjas per partida jassia que sia suspenduda am le huou mays e subtilment escruta am la excoriacio segon la quantitat a tu possibla.
Expose it, and be careful not to cut it; your exposure of it should be done delicately, suspending the testicle more and carefully inspecting it according to the amount possible.

E aprop perfora le ciphac ple de aygua am perforacio ampla, e extratz tota l’aygua.
Then perforate the water-filled sac with a wide opening and extract all the water.

E aprop separa entre doas labias de la seccio am uncis, e exten le ciphac a las partidas desus; e no toques la codena les genetius comprehendent, e inscideys le ciphac en aquela manieyra que es a tu possible.
Separate the two lips of the incision with hooks, and extend the sac to the upper parts; do not touch the covering of the genitals, and cut the sac as much as possible.

E inscideys aquel am la sua totalitat o en pessas, e majorment le sieu latz subtil, quar si tu no perscrutas exquisidament la inscizio de lu, no es fayta segurtat que la aygua no retorne.
Cut it entirely or in pieces, especially its delicate side, because if you do not carefully cut it, there is no guarantee that the water will not return.

Mays si le huou procezeys de aquela defora de la sua codena en la ora de la tua operacio, lahoras quan tu auras complida la seccio del ciphac, retorna dedintz aquel, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la codena dels genetius am sutura, e aprop cura aquel ayssi cum las autras plagua, entro que sia sanat.
But if the testicle comes out of its covering during your operation, once you have completed the incision of the sac, return it inside, and then join the two lips of the genital covering with sutures, and treat it like any other wound until it heals.

E si atrobas le huou corromput per autra malautia, lahoras cove que tu lies les vayssels les quals so sore le suspensori, e extrat le huou, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit.
If you find the testicle is corrupted by another disease, you must tie the vessels on the suspensory cord, remove the testicle, and treat it as previously mentioned.

Mays si l’aygua es agreguada en doas partidas esemps, lahoras sapias que doas son las ernias; donc inscideys aquela partida segon que has feyt en l’autra engualment; e si es a tu vist que sia una opera, lahoras tu la fay.
If the water is accumulated in two separate parts, know that there are two hernias; make the incision in that part as you did in the other; if it appears to be a single operation, then do it.

E aprop tu abstergiys le sanc, e entramet en las seccios lana submersa en oli o en oli rozat; e pausa deforo autra lana la qual tu as submersa en vi e oli, e expandeys aquela sobre dos genetius e·l mirac del ventre; e pausa desobre draps doblatz e pulvils, e lia aquels desobre am liament le qual es segon aquesta forma:
Then cleanse the blood, and place wool soaked in oil or rose oil in the incisions; place other wool soaked in wine and oil outside, spread it over the two genitals and the lower abdomen; place folded cloths and powders on top, and bind them with a bandage in this manner:

e aprop sian preses dos draps e sian humplitz de lana carmenada segon aquesta semblansa; e sian faytas las extremitatz am les quals es premut de coto o de lana humida, e sian agreguatz am strectura en le braguier de las braguas, e la una de las extremitatz prengua del cul entro al dos, e la segonda prengua a la partida del pantenilh, e dos extramitatz sobre dos coyssas dejos e dos extramitatz autras sobre dos angonars, e tota extrictura sia ajustada en le braguier de las braguas.
Take two cloths and fill them with carded wool as follows; make ends of cotton or damp wool, attach them with a structure in the breech of the trousers, one end from the bottom to the back, the second end to the lower part of the abdomen, two ends over the thighs below, and two other ends over the groins, and adjust the whole structure in the breech of the trousers.

E alcunas veguadas aquesta hernia es medicada artificialment am cauteri en loc de seccio am ferr; e es que tu prenguas cauteri cutellar subtil e que inscidas am aquel la codena dels ginitius, e es ignit segon que havem recomtat entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc contenent la aygua, e lahoras tu pren cauteri segon aquesta forma:
Sometimes this hernia is treated artificially with cautery instead of surgical cutting; take a subtle knife-like cautery and incise the covering of the genitals, ignite it as we have described until the white sac containing the water is exposed, then take the cautery in this shape:

e es asemblat a letra greca.
It is shaped like a Greek letter.

E aprop perfora am aquel ciphac, e es ignit entro que tota la humiditat sia fora-gitada.
Then pierce the sac with it, ignite it until all the moisture is expelled.

E aprop exten le ciphac am uncis, e excorja am uncis, e excorja am cauteri subtil ignit; e inscideys aquel segon que es a tu possible entro que eradiques tot lu; e guarda te del huou que·l foc no·l toque.
Extend the sac with hooks, and expose it with hooks, and expose it with a subtle ignited cautery; cut it as much as possible until you eradicate everything; take care not to let the fire touch the testicle.

E sapias que aquesta operacio es pus salva e pus longinqua de flux de sanc, e milhor que operacio am seccio.
Know that this operation is safer and less prone to blood flow, and better than surgery with cutting.

Mays si a tu fa contrarietat apostema caut en la hora de seccio o en hora de cauteri, o flux de sanc, lahoras cove que tu cures qual contrarietat fa a tu per aquo, am curacio la qual conveneys a lu segon que es dit.
But if a hot swelling opposes you during the cutting or cautery operation, or if there is a flow of blood, you must treat the opposition accordingly, with the treatment appropriate for it as mentioned.

Mays si le malaute es pauruc, e no spera la segonda operacio per la sua horribilitat, lahoras administra perforacio segon que yeu recomti aquo; e es quan es certificat deves tu, per aquo que havem dit de las significacios, que aquela hernia es ayguosa.
But if the patient is fearful and does not endure the second operation due to its horror, administer a perforation as I describe here; this is when it is confirmed by you, from what we have said about the signs, that this hernia is watery.

Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute sobre alcuna cezelha elevada, aprop perfora le apostema en la partida pus bassa de lu am spatum lat, e pausa la perforacio segon la longitut del cos.
Then have the patient sit on an elevated seat, pierce the swelling at its lowest part with a broad knife, and make the perforation along the length of the body.

E sia la apercio ampla entro que corro tota l‘aygua.
The opening should be wide enough to drain all the water.

E aprop pausa sobre le loc coto e lia aquel e layssa aquel, per so que corro le romanent de l’aygua.
Then place cotton over the area, bind it, and leave it, so that the remaining water drains.

E aprop cura aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.
Then treat it until the wound is healed.

Mays si contrarietat es a la egrecio de l’aygua en aquela hora tu perforas aquella: e aquo no es fayt sino per aquo quar le pannicol blanc en le orrifici de la plagua fa contrarietat e prohibeys le eyssiment de l’aygua, lahoras cove que tu metas en la plagua pena o instrument am la qual es extrayta l’aygua dels ydropitz, la forma del qual es precedida; o ajusta en la opprecio de la plagua un petit.
But if there is opposition to the drainage of the water when you pierce it, this is because the white membrane in the wound opening opposes and prevents the exit of the water, you must insert a plug or instrument used to extract water from dropsy, as previously described; or adjust a small instrument in the wound opening.

E sapias que l’aygua retorna, e es agueguada aprop vi meses o enaviro aquels; e cum es agreguada, lahoras sia perforat segon aquela meteyssa manieyra, quar le malaute ayssi passara les sieus dias.
Know that the water returns, and it is accumulated around six months or thereabouts; when it is accumulated, pierce it in the same manner, as the patient will thus live out his days.

Capitol .lxiii.
Chapter 63.

De seccio sobre ernia carnosa e la curacio de lu.
On the section about fleshy hernia and its treatment.

Sapias que en la seccio sobre aquesta hernia es temor perdusent a pernicia en las majors disposicios; per que a mi es vista la dimissio de lu e esser salvat per aquella milhor.
Know that in the section on this hernia, there is fear leading to ruin in major cases; therefore, I find that abandoning it and being saved from it is better.

E yeu so rememorant la operacio en aquella e las specias dels apostemas.
I am recalling the operation on it and the types of swellings.

Donc, dic que l‘apostemas natz en les cos dels quals les genetius so conponutz e es fayt aquo per motas causas: o per superfluitat aguda agra, la qual es efundida als genetius, o per percuscio.
I say that the swellings occur in bodies whose genitals are affected and this happens for many reasons: either by an acute sour excess, which is poured into the genitals, or by a blow.

E es la color de la apostema segon la color del cos, e no es atrobat en lu dolor, e es apostema greu.
The color of the swelling matches the body color, and it is not painful, but it is a serious swelling.

E fort leu es apostema lapificada, del qual la color es fosca, e no es centiment a lu.
Often the swelling becomes stone-like, its color is dark, and it has no sensation.

E alcunas veguadas es fayt per nodacio de las arcerias, e per imflacio de aquelas ayssi quo ja es perceubut la rememoracio de lu, o per imflacio de venas.
Sometimes it occurs by blockage of the arteries, and by swelling of them as has already been mentioned, or by swelling of veins.

Mays aquo que es per imflacio de arcerias es conogut per la dispercio de la apostema quan compremas aquella am les tieus ditz; e no cove que aquel toques.
What is caused by swelling of arteries is known by the dispersal of the swelling when you press it with your fingers; it should not be touched.

Mays aquel que es fayt per imflacio de vena no es dispergut de lu alcuna causa deves la compressio am les ditz.
What is caused by swelling of veins is not dispersed at all by compression with fingers.

E ja es possible que sobre aquesta specia sia fayta seccio e sobre les autres carns; e es que tu inscida la codena dels genetius, e aprop esten le huou a las partidas desus, e extratz aquel del ciphac blanc, e deliura le suspensori dels vaysels, e ligua les, e inscideys le suspensori pus que tu deliuras aquel de tota partida de las partidas del huou.
It is possible to make an incision on this type and on other fleshy parts; you must cut the genital covering, extend the testicle to the upper parts, remove it from the white sac, free the suspensory cord from the vessels, tie them, and cut the suspensory cord as you free it from all parts of the testicle.

Donc si l’huou ja es am aquelas carnadas consolida, lahoras cove que tu extraguas le huou e inscidas aquel.
If the testicle is consolidated with those fleshy parts, you must remove and cut it.

E si es adherencia entro alcuna causa del ciphac, o entre aquo que es entre les bayssels, lahoras cove que tu deliures tota aquella adherencia e inscidas aquella per inscizio redonda.
If there is adhesion to any part of the sac, or to the vessels, you must free all that adhesion and cut it with a circular incision.

Mays si es nativitat de carn en le loc de la adherencia la qual es detras, lahoras cove que tu inscidas tot aquo que es de lu, e extraguas le huou ayssi cum havem dit.
If there is a growth of flesh in the place of the adhesion which is behind, you must cut all of it and remove the testicle as we have said.

Donc cum es complida la tua operacio, lahoras omple la plagua de lana imfuza en oli rozat e vi; e aprop cura aquela am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.
When your operation is complete, fill the wound with wool soaked in rose oil and wine; then treat it with the other treatment until it is healed.

Capitol .lxiv.
Chapter 64.

De la curacio de hernia que es de vitz.
On the treatment of hernia caused by veins.

Vit es apostema envolut per alcuna envolucio semblant a broto am mollificacio dels testiculs, e es fayt dificil movement exercitiu e deambulacio sobre le malaute.
Vein swelling is a swelling surrounded by a wrap similar to a shoot with softening of the testicles, making movement, exercise, and walking difficult for the patient.

E en la curacio de aquesta malautia es per temor per aquo del qual es precedida rememoracio.
Treating this illness is feared because of the previously mentioned reasons.

Empero cove que diguam opperacio en aquela segon que fero les primiers.
However, we must describe the operation on it as the first did.

E dic que cove que fassas sezer le malaute sobre una cezelha elevada; e aprop enpelleys le suspensori dels testiculs a las partidas dejos; e aprop te la codena dels genetius am les tieus ditz am les baysels que so probdas a la vergua; e tengua aquels autre ministre que tu, e extenda aquels am extencio vehement.
I say that you should have the patient sit on an elevated seat; push the testicular suspensory to the lower parts; hold the genital covering with your fingers along with the vessels attached to the penis; another assistant should hold and stretch them vehemently.

E aprop inscideys am spatum lat agut per seccio traversa en le dreyt dels vaysels entro que sian les vayssels descubertz.
Then cut with a sharp broad knife transversely over the vessels until they are exposed.

E aprop excorja de tota partida ayssi quo a tu havem dit en extraccio de arceria las quals so en las templas.
Expose all parts as we have described for artery extraction in the temples.

E aprop fica en aquelas un’agulha en la qual sia fiel doble, e lia aquel en le primier del locs en les quals accideys vit, e lia aquel autra veguada en le derier de lor.
Insert a needle with a double thread into them, tie it at the first place where the vein problem occurs, and tie it again at the end of them.

E aprop inscideys aquels en le mieg loc per seccio dreyta segon la longuesa del cos, e extratz aquo que es agreguat de las humiditatz fetulentas e corruptas.
Then cut them in the middle with a straight incision along the length of the body, and remove what is accumulated of fetid and corrupt humors.

E aprop cura la plagua am curacio de las autras plaguas en las quals vols sania esser engendrada per so que caian les vaysels les quals noyreysso un de dos genetius, quar no es mal per aquo.
Then treat the wound as you would other wounds where you want healing to be produced, so that the vessels nourishing one of the two testicles fall off, for there is no harm in this.

Mays si accideys vit a totz les bayssels, lahoras cove que·ls testicols sian extragutz o que les testicols per aquo se cequo am les vayssels, per que sia privat de tot nutriment per la inscizio dels vayssels, e que sian estaborits, o que cequo per so que no sia juvament am aquels.
But if the vein problem affects all the vessels, the testicles must be removed or the testicles and vessels should be closed off, depriving them of all nourishment through vessel incision, and they should be atrophied, or closed off so they are not beneficial.

Capitol lxv.
Chapter 65.

De la cura de hernia entestinal.
On the treatment of intestinal hernia.

Le adveniment de aquesta hernia es per seccio que endeve en le ciphac extendut sobre le ventre de part dels angunars del mirac del ventre, per que deysendo les budels de aquela ruptura ad alcu dels budels.
The occurrence of this hernia is due to a tear that happens in the sac extended over the abdomen from the parts of the inguinal regions, causing the intestines to descend through that rupture to some of the intestines.

E aquesta ruptura es o del ciphac o de excencio de lu, e accideysso aquestas doas specias per motas causas: o percussio, o per sautz, o per clamor, o per elevacio de alcuna causa greu, o per semblantz.
And this rupture is either of the sac or its extension, and these two types occur for many reasons: either from a blow, or a jump, or shouting, or lifting something heavy, or similar.

E·l senhal de aquo, quan es per extencio del ciphac, es que accideys pauc a pauc en lonc temps, e no accideys soptament, e es apostema engual entro ves le preon per so quar le ciphac comprem le budel.
The sign of this, when it is due to an extension of the sac, is that it happens little by little over a long time, and does not happen suddenly, and it is a swelling similar to a tumor because the sac compresses the intestine.

E le senhal de lu es quan es per seccio del ciphac, quar al comensament fa accidir dolor vehement sobtament; e es apostema divers aparent dejos la codena propdana aparent, e aquo es per eyssiment del budel, e·l cos de lu a las partidas deforo del ciphac.
The sign of it is when it is due to a tear in the sac, because initially it causes sudden intense pain; and it is a different swelling apparent below the surface, and this is due to the protrusion of the intestine, with its body outside the sac.

E alcunas veguadas es fora-getat am le budel la tela, e es apelada aquesta hernia entestinal zirbal.
Sometimes the membrane is pushed out with the intestine, and this is called an intestinal hernia with a membrane.

E alcunas veguadas es fayta am ventositat, e alcunas veguadas corr en le budel fenda, e aqui es retenguda, e es am aquo gran pernitia del malaute, e alcunas veguadas fa endevenir dolor malvada e majorment quan es premut.
Sometimes it is formed with gas, and sometimes it runs into the crack of the intestine, where it is retained, causing great harm to the patient, and sometimes it causes severe pain, especially when pressed.

E en la curacio de las especias de aquesta malautia am ferr es temor, per que cove que sia esquivat le cazament en aquela.
And in the treatment of these types of this disease with iron there is fear, so it must be avoided.

E la manieyra de la operacio de aquela es que comandes al malaute que redugua le budel am la sua ma a las partidas dedintz de la sua conquavitat si obezeys al sieu retornament, e aprop sia envessat sobre le sieu col entre las tuas mas, e eleva las cambas de lu.
And the way to perform the operation is to instruct the patient to push the intestine back with his hand into its cavity if it responds to its return, then he should be inverted over his neck between your hands, and you raise his legs.

E aprop sten la codena la qual siec la codena dels testicols a las partidas desus, e inscideys la codena dels testicols tota per le lonc; e aprop fiqua en doas labias de la seccio uncis segon que indigeysses a hubrir la seccio am aquels.
Then stretch the covering that encloses the testicles to the upper parts, and cut the covering of the testicles lengthwise; then place hooks in the two edges of the incision as you need to open the incision with them.

E si’ la seccio segon la quantitat que a tu sia possible que de aquela le huou sia foro-getat.
And if the incision is according to the size that it is possible for you that from there the testicle is pushed out.

E aprop excorja aquela ciphaqueth les quals so dejos la codena dels testicols, entro que sia descubert le ciphac blanc dur de quascuna partida.
Then peel off that sac which is below the covering of the testicles, until the hard white sac is exposed on each side.

Lahoras tu entromet le tieu dit en aquo que siec le testicol, en aquo que es entre ciphac blanc, le qual es dejos la codena del huou, e entre le ciphac segon, e absolve am aquel’adherencia que es en la partida detras del huou.
Then insert your finger into what encloses the testicle, into what is between the white sac, which is below the covering of the testicle, and between the second sac, and release with it the adhesion that is on the back of the testicle.

E aprop mau am la ma la codena dels testicols a las partidas deforo, e am aysso exten le ciphac blanc en sus am la ma sinestra, e eleva le huou am le ciphac a la partida de la seccio; e comanda al ministre que extenda le huou ensus e tu dissolveys la adherencia que es detras am solucio complida.
Then move the covering of the testicles to the outside with your hand, and with that stretch the white sac upwards with your left hand, and lift the testicle with the sac to the incision site; instruct your assistant to stretch the testicle upwards and you dissolve the adhesion that is behind with complete separation.

E cerqua am les tieus ditz que lay no sia alcuna causa del budel envelopat en le ciphac blanc dur.
And check with your fingers that there is no part of the intestine wrapped in the hard white sac.

Mays si tu atrobas de lu alcuna causa, lahoras tu enpelleys aquel al ventre dejos.
But if you find any part of it, then push it back to the abdomen below.

E aprop tu pren una agulha en la qual sia fiel gros fayt de x fiels, e entromet aquel deves le derier del ciphac, le qual es jos la codena dels testicols, la qual siec seccio; e aprop inscideys las extremitatz las quals emineysso del fiel entro que sian quatre fiels, e aprop compausa alcus de lor sobre alcuna figura en manieyra de crotz; e lia am aquel le ciphac del qual havem dit que es dejos la codena dels testicols am fort liament de dos partz.
Then take a needle with a thick thread made of ten threads, and insert it into the back of the sac, which is under the covering of the testicles, which is the incision; then cut the ends that protrude from the thread until there are four threads, then arrange some of them into a cross shape; and tie with it the sac we said is under the covering of the testicles with a strong binding on both sides.

E aprop envolveys las extremitatz dels fiels e lia aquelas am liament vehement entro que alcu dels vayssels que noyrrisso aquels no puscan trametre alcuna causa per so que de aqui no accida apostema caut.
Then wrap the ends of the threads and tie them tightly so that none of the vessels that nourish them can transmit anything, so that no swelling or infection occurs from here.

E pausa autra veguada liament segon foro le primier liament, lonh de lu mens tres ditz; e aprop aquestz dos liaments layssa del ciphac le qual es dejos la codena dels testicols la quantitat de la grandeza del dit, e inscideys tot le romanent segon redondeza, e osta de lu le huou.
And place another binding like the first binding, at least three fingers' width away from it; then leave from the sac, which is under the covering of the testicles, an amount the size of a finger, and cut all the remainder circularly, and remove the testicle.

E aprop inscideys en la partida dejos de la codena dels testicols per seccio de la qual corra sanc e sania ayssi cum havem recomtat en aquo que havem dit.
Then cut the part below the covering of the testicles with an incision from which blood and healing fluid will flow as we have described before.

E aprop aministra lana submersa en oli, e pausa en la plagua; e aministra le liament le qual havem recomtat (e alcunas veguadas le ciphac blanc es cauterizat, le qual havem dit aprop la inscizio de lu temen de flux de sanc, quar motas veguadas accideys aquels) e leyssa le liament entro que per si caia.
Then apply wool soaked in oil, and place it on the wound; and apply the binding we mentioned (and sometimes the white sac is cauterized, as we have said near the incision to prevent blood flow, because this often happens) and leave the binding until it falls off by itself.

Mays si le cazement de lu es tardat, lahoras de aygua cauda sia embrocat, e pausa sobre aquel entro que caia segon que havem dit.
But if its removal is delayed, then it should be soaked with hot water and placed on it until it falls off as we have said.

E aprop cura la plagua am l’autra curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanat.
Then treat the wound with other wound care until it is healed.

Capitol .lxvi.
Chapter 66.

De hernia ventosa.
On windy hernia.

En aquesta hernia no e vist alcu que sia estat ardit sus la curacio de lu am ferr.
In this hernia, no one has been seen to be daring enough to treat it with iron.

E les primiers diyssero que es fayta ayssi cum havem recomtat en la hernia que es am vi; la qual es que tu lies les vayssels aprop la seccio sobre aquela am fecilitat de lu; e aprop secca en le mieg loc en enviro le apostema am aquo que obro aquel, entro que caian les vayssels.
And the first ones said that it is done as we have described in the hernia with life; which is that you tie the vessels near the incision over it easily; then dry the area around the swelling with something that opens it, until the vessels fall off.

E cura la plagua segon que havem dit entro que sia sanada.
And treat the wound as we have said until it is healed.

Capitol .lxvii.
Chapter 67.

De la disropcio que es fayta en les anguonars.
On the rupture that occurs in the groin.

Alcunas veguadas endeve ruptura en les angonars ayssi cum havem dit, e emineys le loc.
Sometimes a rupture occurs in the groin as we have said, and the place swells.

E no deyssen als genetius alcuna causa dels budels al genetius; e si deyssen, aquo es pauc; e retorna s’en en totas horas.
And it does not leave any cause from the intestines to the genitals; and if it does, it is little; and it returns at all times.

Mays si es prolonguat le temps am aquo, es ajustada fissura en le ciphac entro que deysenda le budel en le ciphac; e accideys aquo per la extencio del ciphac le qual es en le angonars ayssi cum havem dit, la qual causa es quar le ciphac es estendut, e aprop es mollificat e·l loc es apostemat e emineys.
But if time is prolonged with this, a fissure is formed in the sac in which the intestine descends into the sac; and this happens because of the extension of the sac that is in the groin as we have said, which causes the sac to be stretched, and then it becomes softened and the place is swollen and enlarged.

E la cura de lu es am cauteri ayssi quo es precedida la narracio de lu.
And the treatment of it is with cautery as previously described.

E alcunas veguadas es curada am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: e es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos entre las tuas mas, e aprop secca le loc de la ruptura dels apostemas emineys am seccio per la latitut segon la quantitat de tres ditz.
And sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner: and the patient lies on his back between your hands, then dry the place of the rupture from the swelling with an incision across it according to the width of three fingers.

E aprop strenh le ciphac blanc que es jos la codena entro que sia descubert.
Then stretch the white sac that is under the covering until it is exposed.

E aprop pren le ray e pausa aquel sobre le loc eminent del ciphac, e prem aquel al preon del ventre.
Then take a rod and place it on the swollen area of the sac, and press it to the belly button.

E aprop cus le dos locs eminentz sobre la extremitat del ray del ciphac, e ajusta am la sutura un de aquels am l’autre.
Then sew the two swollen areas over the end of the rod of the sac, and join them with the suture.

E aprop extratz la extremitat del ray, e no inscidas del ciphac de tot, ni no extenda le huou, ni autra causa ayssi cum yeu te fi saber en la curacio de hernia entestinal.
Then remove the end of the rod, and do not cut the sac completely, nor extend the testicle, nor any other part as I let you know in the treatment of intestinal hernia.

E aprop cura aquela am la curacio de las plaguas, e cum inscideyses les fiels, mundifica aquela e restaura la plagua entro que sia consolidada; quar le ciphac es contrayt e no es ajustada la eminencia de ruptura.
Then treat it with wound care, and when you cut the threads, clean it and restore the wound until it is healed; because the sac is contracted and the rupture is not swollen.

E cauteri es milhor en aquest loc, quar es pus propda a salut.
And cautery is better in this place, because it is closer to health.

Capitol .lxviii.
Chapter 68.

De mollificacio de la codena dels testiculs.
On the softening of the covering of the testicles.

Motas veguadas la codena dels testiculs en alcus homes es mollificada per aysso quar las carns que so entre aquela son mollificadas, e es fedat le reguardament de lu.
Sometimes the covering of the testicles in some men is softened because the flesh between it is softened, and its care is unpleasant.

Adonc necessari es ad aquel que es preguat en la curacio de lu que fassa jazer le malaute segon le sieu dos, e enscida tota la codena la qual es mollificada sobre la codena natural; e aprop que ajuste doas labias am la sutura.
Then it is necessary for the one who is asked to treat it to make the patient lie on his back, and cut all the covering that is softened over the natural covering; then join the two edges with the suture.

E si vols, cus en le comensament la superfluitat de la codena mollificada am tres cozeduras o quatre e am ferma sutura.
And if you want, sew at the beginning the excess of the softened covering with three or four stitches and a firm suture.

E aprop inscideys entre las suturas; e aprop cura per curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat e caian les fiels.
Then cut between the sutures; and then treat it as with other wounds until it is healed and the threads fall off.

Capitol .lxix.
Chapter 69.

De castracio.
On castration.

Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias.
You should know that castration in our law is excommunicated, but for a reason it is allowed for me to remember it in this book; and its remembrance is necessary only for two reasons, one is so that it is in the knowledge of the doctor when asked about it, that he knows the treatment for the one it happens to; and the other reason is that we often need to castrate other animals for our benefit, such as horses, goats, pigs, and similar animals.

E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.
So I say that castration is done in two ways: either by attrition, or by incision and cutting.

Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.
But in the one that is done by attrition, the way of the operation is that we make the animal sit in hot water until its genitals are softened and relaxed and hang down.

E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.
Then take them in your hand until they are dissolved and do not appear under touch.

Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.
But in castration done by incision and cutting, you need to hold the animal and press the covering of its testicles with your left hand.

E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.
Then tie the suspensory, and cut over each testicle with an incision until both testicles protrude.

E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.
Then cut those more that you have exposed.

E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.
And do not leave any part of the sac on them, except the subtle sac that is over the bases.

E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.
And this manner of castration is better than the one done by attrition, because strong attrition leaves some part of the testicles that causes the animal to desire mating.

E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.
Then treat the wound until it is healed.

Capitol .lxx.
Chapter 70.

De la cura de hermafrodozia.
On the treatment of hermaphroditism.

Hermafrodozia en les homes es segon dos manieyras: la una es quar o appar en aquo que siec l’espazi en la codena de testiculs, en aquel que es entre dos testiculs figura quar cunh de femna en la qual so pels.
Hermaphroditism in men is in two ways: one is when it appears in the space in the covering of the testicles, in that between the two testicles there is a figure like a female vulva in which there is hair.

E alcunas veguadas de aquel corr urina le qual es en la codena dels testiculs.
And sometimes from it flows urine which is in the covering of the testicles.

Mays en las femnas es una specia: e es que·l conh de la femna sobre le pentenilh es ayssi cum dos testiculs de home un pauc de tot yminiheys a la partida deforo ayssi cum le perpucii de home e dos testicols.
But in women it is one type: and it is that the vulva of the woman above the pubis is like two testicles of a man a little extending outward like the foreskin of a man and two testicles.

E la curacio es de tres specias: de dos dels homes e de una specia de las femnas.
And the treatment is of three types: two for men and one type for women.

E es que cove que tu inscidas aquelas carns ajustadas entro que efuga la emprecio de aquela, e aprop que cures aquelas am curacio de las autras plaguas.
And it is that you need to cut those attached flesh until the appearance of it is removed, then treat them with wound care.

E en la segonda specia dels homes de la qual yeys urina la qual es en la codena dels testiculs, no es curacio ni opperacio en lu.
And in the second type in men from which urine flows that is in the covering of the testicles, there is no treatment or operation for it.

Capitol .lxxi.
Chapter 71.

De lentinge e de carn eminent per causas de las femnas.
On lentigo and protruding flesh from causes in women.

Lentige fort leu es ajustada sobre causas naturals entro que es etressat e es fayt leg le reguardament; e alcunas veguadas es magnificada en alcunas femnas en tant entro que es spandit ayssi cum en les homes e perve entro al coito.
Lentigo is often joined to natural causes when it is stressed and made the target of attention; and sometimes it is enlarged in some women to the extent that it spreads like in men and becomes involved in intercourse.

Adonc cove que tu tenguas la superfluitat de lentinge am la tua ma o am unci e inscidas.
Then you need to hold the excess of lentigo with your hand or with a hook and cut it.

E no ultimes en inscizio, majorment en le preon de la razit, per so que no endevengua flux de sanc.
And do not delay in cutting, especially at the base of the root, so that it does not cause a flow of blood.

E aprop cura aquela am curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanada.
Then treat it with wound care until it is healed.

Mays carn nascuda es carn que nays en le horrifici de la mayre entro que umple aquel, e fort leu es eyssit a las partidas deforo segon semblansa de coa (e per aquo alscus primiers appelero aquo “malautia caudada”); donc cove que nos inscidam ayssi cum inscidem lentinge, e curem aquela entro que sia sanada.
But new flesh is flesh that grows in the orifice of the mother until it fills it, and often it is expelled to the outside in the form of a tail (and for this reason some first called it "tailed disease"); so we need to cut it as we cut lentigo, and treat it until it is healed.

Capitol .lxxii.
Chapter 72.

De curacio de alratica.
On the treatment of imperforate hymen.

Alratica es que le conh de la femna no sia perforat, o sia le trauc petit.
Alratica is when the vulva of the woman is not perforated or the opening is very small.

E es o natural o accidental.
And it is either natural or accidental.

Accidental es per malautia la qual ha precedit, e aquela es fayta o per carn nada ajustada o per ciphac subtil o espes.
Accidental is due to a preceding illness, and it is caused either by flesh grown together or by a thin or thick membrane.

E es fayt o en le preon de la mayre, o en les costatz de lu, o en le pus sobira de lu, o en le pus bas de lu, e prohibeys de cuoyt e de enprenguacio e de enfantament, e fort leu prohibeys las mestruas.
And it happens either at the base of the vagina, or on its sides, or at its top, or at its bottom, and it prevents intercourse, conception, and childbirth, and often stops menstruation.

E la cognicio de aquela es fayta per reguardament de la metrona, si la oppilacio es apparent, propdana; mays si no es apparent, lahoras tu cerqua aquela am les tieus ditz o am le ray.
And the diagnosis of this is made by the observation of the midwife if the blockage is apparent and near; but if it is not apparent, then you search for it with your fingers or with a rod.

Mays si oppilacio es per ciphac subtil, e es propda a las doas labias, lahoras tu coyta e disromp aquela.
But if the obstruction is due to a thin membrane and it is near the two labia, then you cut it and break it.

E es que pauses sobre las doas labias pulvils, e aprop pausa les tieus ditz indicz de amdoas las mas encemps.
And it is that you place on the two labia some powder, and then place your index fingers of both hands together.

E la femna sia sobre le sieu dos, las sieuas coyssas extendudas, e aprop exten las doas labias am forsa entro que aquel ciphac subtil sia romput e la oppilacio sia uberta.
And the woman should be on her back, her thighs extended, and then extend the two labia with force until the thin membrane is broken and the obstruction is opened.

E aprop pren lana e enbeu le en oli e pausa aquela sobre·l loc, e jagua am home le dia per so que·l loc inscis no sia consolidat.
Then take wool and soak it in oil and place it on the spot, and lie with a man that day so that the cut place does not heal.

Mays si le ciphac es gros e espes, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquel am spatum lat o am fuelha de mirta.
But if the membrane is thick and dense, then you need to cut it with a broad spatula or a myrtle leaf.

Mays si la oppilacio es per carnada, lahoras suspen aquela am unci, e inscideys aquela.
But if the obstruction is due to grown flesh, then lift it with a hook, and cut it.

E sian am tu las medicinas que fan cessar flux de sanc ses mordicacio, ayssi cum ahacatia, e sanc de drago, e enses, ajustat am album de huou.
And have with you the medicines that stop the flow of blood without stinging, such as acacia, dragon's blood, and frankincense, mixed with egg white.

E aprop aministra una canulha de plom ampla per so que la plagua no sia consolidada leugierament.
Then administer a broad lead tube so that the wound does not heal quickly.

E tengua aquela per alcus jorns e aministra calgua de li sec.
And keep it for some days and administer dry calk.

E aprop sia curada am l’autra curacio de consolidacio entro que sia sanada.
Then treat it with other wound care until it is healed.

E alcunas vetz accideys en la mayre nativitat de altres carns, e lahoras cove que inscidas segon aquesta manieyra.
And sometimes there is a birth of other flesh in the vagina, and then you need to cut it in this manner.

Mays si aysso es per apostema crancos, a l’apostema crancos le qual es en la mayre no sia fayta contrarietat am ferr en deguna manieyra.
But if this is due to a cancerous abscess, no treatment with iron should be done to the cancerous abscess in the vagina in any way.

Capitol .lxxiii.
Chapter 73.

De la cura de emorroydas e de tayl e de botor roja que accideysso en le conh de las femnas.
On the treatment of hemorrhoids and warts and red swelling that occur in the vulva of women.

Emorroydas so apprecio dels orificis de motas venas entro que de aquellas corro mot sanc continuadament; e cum so antiquadas emorroydas e son fayts theyls.
Hemorrhoids are seen at the openings of many veins from which much blood continuously flows; and when hemorrhoids are old, warts are formed.

E ja yeu he dit en la divisio las specias de aquellas e les senhals de aquellas, e diyre ayssi aquelas que recebo curacio e aquelas que no recebo curacio.
And I have already mentioned in the division the types of these and their signs, and I will also say which of these can be treated and which cannot be treated.

Donc dic que emorroydas e theyls quan so en le preon de la mayre e no apparo al sentiment, lahoras en aquellas no sia fayta curacio am ferr.
So I say that hemorrhoids and warts when they are at the base of the vagina and are not felt, then no treatment with iron should be done for those.

Mays aquellas las quals so en le orrifici de la mayre sobre las quals catz sentiment, so aquellas que so curadas.
But those which are in the opening of the vagina and are felt, those are the ones that are treated.

E cove que tu metas la femna en mayso frega e aprop exten atheyl am les forfexs, o am drap aspre, e inscideys aquellas am las razitz.
And you need to place the woman in a warm bath and then extend the hemorrhoid with forceps, or with rough cloth, and cut them at the roots.

E aprop pulveriza sobre aquellas deves le fluxs del sanc de una de las polveras insciscivas ses mordicacio, ayssi cum acassia e semblant ad aquels.
Then sprinkle on them some of the powders that stop bleeding without stinging, such as acacia and similar ones.

E aprop enpellesca les sieus pes per una hora, e aprop pausa aquela en aygua freja.
Then bind her feet together for an hour, and then place her in cold water.

E si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras fay aquella sezer en decoccio de sumat e de scorsas de milgranas e de gualas e de semblantz.
And if the bleeding persists, then make her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peels and galls and similar things.

E aprop pren farina de ordi e comfiys aquella am miel e vi agre e fay emplastre am aquo sobre le dos de lu.
Then take barley flour and mix it with honey and sour wine and make a plaster with it over the back of the area.

E si le sanc es abscindit, bo es; e sino, fay adherir am dos ventozas, e a las mamilhas ses escarificatio.
And if the bleeding stops, it is good; if not, use two cupping glasses, and on the breasts without scarification.

E aprop pren lana e submergeys aquela am suc de coliandre o am suc de arnagloza o am suc de guarravier am vi pentit e fay adherir al loc; e aprop cura le loc am enguentz entro que sia sanat.
Then take wool and soak it in coriander juice or nightshade juice or rockrose juice with sour wine and apply it to the place; then treat the place with ointments until it is healed.

Mays athyl rog le qual es de aspre reguardament, cove que tu inscidas aquo que a tu appar de aquel segon que he dit en theyl engualment.
But a red wart which is of rough appearance, you need to cut that which appears to you of it as I have said in the treatment of hemorrhoids.

E cura aquel entro que sia sanat.
And treat it until it is healed.

Capitol .lxxiv.
Chapter 74.

De perforacio de eyssedura accident en la mayre.
On perforation of accidental abscess in the vagina.

Motas specias de apostemas accideysso en la mayre, ayssi cum cranc e apostema lapident e ulceracios e adhubelat e erpetromens e fistulas emorroyas e raguarrias e thyl e autres apostemas.
Many types of abscesses occur in the vagina, such as cancer, stone abscess, ulcers, swollen tissues, herpes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, cracks, warts, and other abscesses.

E yeu ja he dit aquestas malautias e las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e las curacios de lor en la divisio.
And I have already mentioned these diseases and their types and their signs, and their treatments in the division.

E cove que yeu digua en aquest tractat de apostema caut le qual ve en la mayre quan es dels apostemas que collegeysso sania, e si vols saber en qual manieyra se fa la opperacio de lu am ferr.
And I need to say in this treatise about the hot abscess which comes in the vagina when it is one of the abscesses that collects pus, and if you want to know in what manner the operation of it is done with iron.

Adonc cove que tu consideres si la dolor de la apostema en le sieu comensament es aguda am percussio e flecma e febre, e vezes aquel enrogezir e si catz sobre aquel le sentiment, lahoras no·t coytes am perforacio de lu, e cura aquel am aquo que ajuda sobre la maturacio entro que cesse la acuitat dels accidentz.
Then you need to consider if the pain of the abscess in its beginning is sharp with throbbing and phlegm and fever, and if you see it redden and if it is felt, then do not hurry with its perforation, and treat it with what helps with maturation until the acuteness of the symptoms stops.

E lahoras cove que tu fassas cezer la femna sobre una cezelha que aia doas cezelhas; e recline sobre le sieu dos e ajusta les sieus pes a la partida pus dejos del ventre, e las sieus coyssas sian expandudas, e pausa les sieus brasses dejos les sieus denols, e lia quascus am liament ad aquo convenient.
And then you need to make the woman sit on a chair that has two seats; and recline on her back and adjust her feet to the lower part of the abdomen, and her thighs should be spread, and place her arms under her knees, and tie each with a band to something convenient.

E aprop la matrona segua del latz dreyt e aministre le instrument am le qual es ubert le orrifici de la mayre, la forma del qual vindra en aquelas causas que·s faran aprop.
Then the midwife stands on the right side and administers the instrument with which the vaginal opening is opened, the shape of which will be shown in those cases that will be performed next.

E cove quan vols ministrar aquest instrument que tu fiques am lo ray le preon de la mayre de la femna, e aquo que del instrument es intrat en la mayre no sia mays que·l preon de la mayre e leda le malaute.
And when you want to use this instrument, you need to place the base of the vagina of the woman with the rod, and what is inserted from the instrument into the vagina should not be more than the base of the vagina and harm the patient.

Mays si l’estrument es major que·l preon de la mayre, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils sobre la textura del preon de la mayre per sso que sia prohibit l’intrament de tot instrument en le preon de la mayre.
But if the instrument is larger than the base of the vagina, then you need to place powders on the tissue of the base of the vagina so that the entrance of any instrument into the base of the vagina is prevented.

E cove que tu pauses le vertitge que corr en le strument del latz pus desus e que le ministre tengua le strument e revolva le vertitge entro que sia ubert le orrifici de la mayre.
And you need to place the screw that runs in the instrument from the top side and the administrator holds the instrument and turns the screw until the vaginal opening is open.

E cum appar la excitura, e es tocada am la ma e es leon e molh, lahoras cove que tu secces aquela deves le cap de lu am spatum lat.
And when the abscess appears, and it is felt by the hand and is smooth and soft, then you need to cut it from its head with a broad spatula.

E cum la sania es evacuada, lahoras cove que tu pauses en la plagua una meca submersa en oli rozat o oli vert en le qual sia alcuna stiptisitat; e pausa la calca7 en la seccio en le preon de la mayre.
And when the pus is evacuated, then you need to place in the wound a swab soaked in rose oil or green oil in which there is some astringency; and place the swab in the section in the base of the vagina.

E pause deforo la mayre e sobre le pentenilh lana munda submersa en aygua en la qual sian bulidas malvas.
And place outside the vagina and on the pubis clean wool soaked in water in which mallows have been boiled.

E aprop sia curada aprop dos dias am enguent le qual conveneys ad aquo entro que sia sanat.
Then treat it for two days with ointment that is suitable for this until it is healed.

E alcunas veguadas es lavada la mayre e la plagua enayssi que es cristerisat am aygua e mel, e aprop am aygua en la qual es bulhida razit de liri o de aristologia longua, e aprop retorna al enguent.
And sometimes the vagina and the wound are washed so that it is crystallized with water and honey, and then with water in which lily root or long aristolochia is boiled, and then return to the ointment.

E si la plagua es dedintz en la mayre ameguada, lahoras cove que tu sias prohibit de la curacio de lu am ferr, habantz cura aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio.
And if the wound is deep in the vagina and hidden, then you should be prohibited from treating it with iron, but treat it with what we have said in the division.

Capitol .lxxv.
Chapter 75.

A ensenhar las matronas en qual manieyre les enbrios bius sian medicatz quan yeysso segon figura no-natural.
To teach the midwives in what manner the live embryos are treated when they come out in an unnatural position.

Necessaria causa es que la matrona conogua en le comensament la figura del enfantament natural per senhals de lu, e es que quan tu vezas la femna expremar a las partidas dejos e desira odorar le ayre, e sobre aquo es enleujada per aquo que sobre ela es del part, e festina le eyssiment del enbrio, lahoras sapias que aquest part es segon figura natural, e es l’eyssiment de lu sobre le sieu cap, e la segondina am aquel o suspensa o pendent del ombelic.
It is necessary that the midwife knows at the beginning the figure of natural childbirth by its signs, and when you see the woman exerting pressure on her lower parts and wanting to breathe the air, and then she is relieved by the pressure of the childbirth, and hastens the emergence of the embryo, then know that this birth is according to the natural position, and it is the emergence of the baby on its head, and the placenta with it or hanging or suspended from the umbilical cord.

Donc cum tu vezes aquels senhals, lahoras cove que·l ventre de lu sia compremut per so que l’embrio deysenda leugerament quar quan deyssen sobre le sieu cap, deysen a lu la segondina, e es mondada de aquelas superfluitatz am bona mondificacio.
So when you see these signs, you need to compress the belly so that the embryo descends gently because when it descends on its head, it descends with the placenta, and it is cleaned of those superfluities with good cleansing.

Mays aquel que es otra aquest part es no-natural e no-lausable, quar quan le enbrio es eyssit sobre sos pes e·l cos de lu es eyssit devant le cap de lu e·ls pes de lu, e la ma de lu una, o al pe de lu .i., o es eyssit le cap de lu e la ma de lu, o al ventre de lu, e fort leu es convertit sobre le sieu col, e semblant de las figuras de lu no-lausablas.
But the one that is different from this birth is unnatural and not praiseworthy, because when the embryo comes out on its feet and its body comes out before its head and its feet, and one of its hands, or on its foot, or its head and its hand come out, or its belly, and it is very easily twisted on its neck, and such shapes are not praiseworthy.

Don necessaria causa es a la matrona que sia savia e subtil en totas aquelas causas, e que·s guarde de error e de decepcio.
Therefore, it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in all these cases and to avoid error and deception.

E yeu so mostrant tota figura de aquelas, e qual engen es en aquelas per so que sia significat per aquo e sia stat sobre aquo.
And I am showing each figure of these, and what tool is used in them so that it is indicated by this and it is established accordingly.

Quan le feyt es eyssit sobre le sieu cap per egrecio natural, e aquel es vehement sobre la femna e es fayt a lu part dificil, e vezes la vertut de lu ja debelitada, lahoras fay aquela sezer, o que las femnas tenguan lu, e evapora le conh de lu am fenugrec coyt e am olis humitz.
When the baby comes out on its head by natural expulsion, and this is strong on the woman and makes the birth difficult, and sometimes her strength is already weakened, then make her sit, or the women hold her, and vaporize her vagina with boiled fenugreek and moist oils.

E aprop entrometa la metrona entre les sieus ditz espatum petit e fenda am aquel la segondina, o secce aquela am la sua ungla entro que corro aquo que es en ela de humiditat.
And then the midwife inserts between her fingers a small spatula and cuts with it the placenta, or cuts it with her nail until the moisture within it flows out.

E preme le ventre de la femna entro que deyssenda le fet.
And press the woman's belly until the fetus descends.

Mays si no deyssen, lahoras cove que la femna sia cristirizada de mucellage de ptilli e mucellage de fenugrec am cizami.
But if it does not descend, then the woman needs to be anointed with a mucilage of psyllium and fenugreek with sesame.

E aprop comanda a lu, aprop le cristeri, que sia compremuda e fay aquela stornudar am condisi; e te la boca de lu e·l nas de lu per huna hora, quar le fet sira foro-getat tantost.
And then instruct her, near the anointing, to be compressed and make her sneeze with a condition; and hold her mouth and nose for an hour, because the fetus will be expelled quickly.

E si las doas mas del fet so foro-getadas al comensament, lahoras cove que tu redusiscas aquelas am fecilitat petit a petit.
And if both hands of the fetus are expelled at the beginning, then you need to reduce them easily little by little.

Mays si no obezeys al intrament, lahoras pausa la femna sobre una cezelha e leva les pes de lu sus, e aprop concuceys la cezelha sobre la terra; e la femna sia tenguda que no caia deves la concussio.
But if it does not respond to insertion, then place the woman on a chair and lift her feet up, and then shake the chair on the ground; and the woman should be held so that she does not fall due to the shaking.

E si las mas no son dedintz tornadas e morr le fet, lahoras inscideys aquelas e extratz le romament del fet o lia le cors a la ma de lu am drap e extratz aquel am equalitat, quar aquel sira foro-getat.
And if the hands are not turned inside and the fetus dies, then cut them and extract the remainder of the fetus or tie its body to the hand with a cloth and extract it with equal force, because it will be expelled.

De eyssiment del embrio sobre les sieus pes.
About the emergence of the embryo on its feet.

Quan le fet yeys sobre les sieus pes, lahoras cove que tu impelliscas aquels en sus, e aprop convertas le fet petit, e aprop que engualhes aquel, e aprop que prenguas un pe de lu e extendas aquels petit a petit.
When the fetus comes out on its feet, then you need to push them up, and then turn the fetus gently, and then straighten it, and then take one of its feet and extend it little by little.

Mays cum son eyssit entro a las coyssas, lahoras tu comanda a lu que se exprema, e fay aquela extornudar am condizi, quar sira foro-getat si Deus lo vol.
But when it is out to the thighs, then you instruct her to exert pressure, and make her sneeze with a condition, because it will be expelled if God wills.

E si no es foro-getat am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras tu retorna le fet petit a petit entro que pauses aquel segon figura natural, quar aquel sira lahoras foro-getat am leugier eyssiment.
And if it is not expelled with what we have recommended, then you return the fetus little by little until you place it in the natural position, because then it will be expelled with an easy emergence.

E si es prohibit am tot aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras pren de musellage de altea e de goma dissolvuda, e percuteys tot en le mortier per bona percussio, e aprop linieys am aquo le conh de la femna, el pus bas del ventre de lu.
And if it is prohibited with all that we have recommended, then take mucilage of mallow and dissolved gum, and pound it all in a mortar with good pounding, and then anoint the woman’s vagina and the lower part of her belly with it.

E aprop fay aquela cezer en aygua tebeza, entro que consegua les ypocondias.
And then make her sit in warm water, until it reaches her hypochondria.

E cum vezes que las partidas dejos de lu so lenificadas, lahoras fay a lu subfumiguacio de mirta e sub-pausa aquela a lu.
And when you see that her lower parts are softened, then make her inhale the smoke of myrtle and place her over it.

E quan te la sub-fumiguacio per una hora, lahoras tu la fay sezer sobre una cezelha, e aprop fay aquela stornudar e extrenh la boca de lu, e levas de aquela, e prem la partida pus bassa del ventre de lu am leugiera compressio, quar le fet sira tantost foro-getat.
And when she has inhaled the smoke for an hour, then make her sit on a chair, and then make her sneeze and stretch her mouth, and lift her from it, and press the lower part of her belly with light compression, because the fetus will be quickly expelled.

Eyssiment del fet sobre les sieus denols e las suas mas.
Emergence of the fetus on its knees and hands.

Quan le fet eyssira segon aquesta forma, lahoras tu engenies en entrometen las suas mas petit a petit; e aprop la femna stia evessada sobre le sieu col, e les pes de lu pengo en jos, e aquelas sia jasent sobre le lieyt, e complegua las suas mas.
When the fetus emerges in this form, then you need to handle it by inserting your hands little by little; and then make the woman bend over on her neck, and her feet hang down, and she lies on the bed, and hold her hands together.

E aprop prem sobre le ventre de lu petit a petit, e aprop extratz aquo que es dejos les pes de lu de las aurelhas entro que sia preparada en la partida pus dejos.
And then press on her belly little by little, and then extract what is under her feet from the ears until it is prepared in the lower part.

E si le fet no es fora-getat, lahoras pren les pes de lu e mau aquels am movement vehement, e aprop prem aquo que es sobre les ypocondres petit a petit entro que le fet puege a las partidas desus.
And if the fetus is not expelled, then take her feet and shake them with strong movement, and then press what is over her hypochondria little by little until the fetus rises to the upper parts.

E aprop entrometa las suas mas e engualhe le fet petit a petit, e comanda a la femna que se exprema entro que le fet sia foro-getat.
And then insert your hands and straighten the fetus little by little, and instruct the woman to exert pressure until the fetus is expelled.

Eyssiment del fet latutidinalment pendent una de las suas mas.
Emergence of the fetus laterally with one of its hands hanging.

Sia engeniat en reduccio de la ma de lu, mays si no podes aquela reducir, lahoras eleva la femna e fe aquella anar.
It needs to be handled by reducing the hand, but if you cannot reduce it, then lift the woman and make her walk.

E si anar no pot, lahoras fay la jazer sobre le lieyt, e concuteys las coyssas de lu am concussio vehement, e aprop aministra liamentz les quals yeu e recomtatz de mucillages.
And if she cannot walk, then make her lie on the bed, and shake her thighs with strong shaking, and then administer the mucilages I have mentioned.

E si es vengut le enfantament, lahoras fay aquela sezer sobre cezelha, e aprop studia sobre la reduccio de la ma, e enguala le fet segon figura natural, e fay stornudar la femna e comanda a lu que comprema a si entro que sia foro-getat.
And if the childbirth comes, then make her sit on a chair, and then study the reduction of the hand, and straighten the fetus according to the natural position, and make the woman sneeze and instruct her to exert pressure until it is expelled.

Eyssiment del fet sobre·l col expandudas las suas mas e la fassia de lu es al dos de la sua mayre.
Emergence of the fetus on its neck with its hands spread and its face to its mother’s back.

Cove que la matrona tengua la ma del fet e aprop revolva aquel petit a petit, e eque aquel am facilitat.
The midwife needs to hold the fetus's hand and then turn it little by little, and align it easily.

E cum es e quant so es engualhat, e lahoras pausa sobre le conh de lu aquo que havem recomtat de oli e de mucillages.
And when it is aligned, then place on her vagina what we have recommended of oil and mucilages.

E aprop comandas a lu que·s maugua petit a petit, e quan auras feyt aquo, lahoras fay aquela cezer sobre una cezelha e comanda li que sia inclinada sobre le latz dreyt, e aprop comanda a lu que sia compremuda; e fay aquela stornudar am condizi.
And then instruct her to move little by little, and when you have done this, then make her sit on a chair and instruct her to lean to the right side, and then instruct her to be compressed; and make her sneeze with a condition.

Exitus foetus praeparati super latus.
Exit of the fetus prepared on its side.

Quan deyssen a horrifici de la mayre segon aquesta manieyra, considera, e lahoras tu inscideys la segondina am la tua ungla entro que sia evacuada de la humiditat.
When it descends to the horror of the mother in this manner, consider, and then you cut the placenta with your nail until the moisture is evacuated.

E si le fet es suspendut sobre la cara e·l col de lu, lahoras tu inscideys aquela del embelic, per so que no sia retengut e mora.
And if the fetus is suspended on its face and neck, then you cut it from the umbilical cord, so that it is not retained and dies.

E aprop empelleys le fet a las partidas dedintz entro que pauses aquel segon que cove, e manda a la femna que comprema a si alcunas veguadas, e el sira fora-getat am eyssiment leugier, si Dieus o vol.
And then push the fetus inside until you place it as needed, and instruct the woman to exert pressure a few times, and it will be expelled with easy emergence, if God wills.

Exitus geminorum aut foetuum multorum.
Exit of twins or multiple fetuses.

Sapias que gemels motas veguadas so natz, e alcunas vetz naysso tres o quatre, mays aquo es estranh e tart s’endeve; mays v so causas foro natura, e no vivo.
Know that twins are often born, and sometimes three or four are born, but this is rare and seldom happens; but sometimes they are born by nature, and not alive.

E conte aquelas, ja sia que sian montiplicatz, una segondina, e son seperatz per ciphac, distingen aquels enter le liguament en l’ombilic de cascun de aquels E alcunas veguadas so foro-getatz ayssi cum es un fet per eyssiment natural leugier, e so eysitz alcunas veguadas per eyssiment no-lausabla ayssi cum havem recomtat.
And count them, even if they are multiplied, with one placenta, and they are separated by a membrane, distinguishing them by the ligament in the umbilical cord of each of them. And sometimes they are expelled just like a fetus with easy natural emergence, and sometimes they are expelled with an unnatural emergence as we have recounted.

E si son dificils alcus de lor deves le enfantament e perveno ad aquo que havem dit de las figuras no-naturals, lahoras tu cura aquels ayssi cum havem recontat.
And if some of them are difficult during childbirth and come to what we have said about the unnatural figures, then you treat them as we have recounted.

E si’ la matrona subtil e fassa aquo que fa am facilitat e subtilitat, e am tarditat, e sia ingeniat segon tota figura segon que es a lu preparat de l’engen amenant a salut.
And if the midwife is subtle and does this with ease and subtlety, and with delay, and is skilled in every figure as it is prepared with the skill bringing health.

Rememoratio eius quod formatur in matrice ex embrionibus et Abortiuntur.
Remembrance of what is formed in the womb from embryos and aborted.

Alcunas veguadas son formatz en la mayre un, e dos, e tres, e quatre, e v, e vi, e vii, e mays x, e ja es deves mi verificat que una femna abortem ne getet vi, e una autra x totz formatz, la qual causa fo fayta per mensuracio dels glorios savis.
Sometimes one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, or even ten are formed in the mother, and it has been verified by me that a woman aborted and expelled six, and another ten all formed, which was done by the measurement of the glorious sages.

E tot aysso cove que sia en la sciencia de la matrona quar fort leu ad aquela parve semblant de aquo, e donc opause se ad aquo am so que cove.
And all this must be in the knowledge of the midwife because very soon she will encounter such a case, and therefore she should act accordingly with what is appropriate.

Capitol .lxxvi.
Chapter 76

De extraccio del fet quan es mort.
On extracting the fetus when it is dead.

Quan tu curas le fet mort am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la medicacio e no es defora eyssit, e tu yest forsat usar de opperacio am ma, lahoras cove que consideras si la femna es de sana vertut e no es am alcu dels accidentz per les quals sobre ela es temuda perdicio.
When you treat the dead fetus with what we have discussed in the section on medication and it has not come out, and you are forced to use manual operation, then you must consider if the woman is of healthy constitution and not afflicted with any conditions that could lead to her demise.

Lahoras cove que la femna sia envessada sobre le lieyt sobre le sieu dos, e sia le cap de lu enclinat enjos e las coyssas de lu sian elevadas.
Then, the woman must be laid on her back on the bed, with her head inclined downwards and her thighs elevated.

E·l ministre tengua aquela de doas partz o sia liada en le lieyt per so que·l cos de lu no se extenda deves la extraccio del fet.
And the assistant should hold her from both sides or tie her to the bed so that her body does not move during the extraction of the fetus.

E aprop tu humecta la boca de la mayre de lu am olis humitz e am mucellage de altea e de fenugrec e de semensa de li.
Then, you should moisten the mother's genital area with humid oils and mucilage of mallow, fenugreek, and linseed.

E aprop unte la matrona la sua ma am aquels olis e mucellages, e aprop entrometa la sua ma am fecilitat en la mayre, e aprop cerque am la ma loc en le qual fique les uncis en le fet.
Next, the midwife should anoint her hand with these oils and mucilages, and then gently insert her hand into the mother, searching with her hand for a place to hook onto the fetus.

E locs convenient en aquo: adonc tu considera si le fet es preparat que deysenda sobre le sieu cap, e lahoras tu fique les uncis en les huels de lu, o en le col, o en la boca, o en le palat, o dejos la barba, o en la furcula de lu, o en les locs propdas de las costas, o dejos les ypocondres.
And appropriate places for this are: if the fetus is positioned to come out head first, then you should hook into its eyes, or the neck, or the mouth, or the palate, or under the chin, or in the collarbone area, or in the spaces near the ribs, or under the hypochondria.

Mays si le deysendiment es sobre les pes de lu, lahoras en le pentenilh, o en le mieg de las costas.
But if it is positioned feet first, then in the groin, or in the middle of the back.

E cove que tengua le unci am la ma dreyta, e pausa la curvitat de lu en aquel loc le qual es entre les ditz de la ma senestra, e entrometa la ma am facilitat e fique le unci en alcu de aquels locs les quals havem ditz, entro que pervengua a la causa boyda.
And you must hold the hook with your right hand, place the curved part of it between the fingers of your left hand, and gently insert your hand and place the hook in one of those mentioned locations until you reach the empty cause.

E aprop pause e fique en la apposicio de lu un autre unci, o le tertz si es necessitat, per so que sia atraccio engual, e no sia extencio segon la sua rectetut tant solament.
And then place and fix another hook, or a third if needed, so that the traction is equal and not just in one direction.

Ans sia maugut a tota partida, per so que l’eyssiment de lu sia alleujat ayssi cum es fayt en dent deves la eradicacio de lu.
Rather, it should be pulled in all directions, so that its extraction is eased, just as it is done when removing a tooth from its socket.

E cove en lu aquo que es entre lor que la extencio sia mollificada; e si alcuna partida de lu es retenguda, lahoras cove que la matrona unte alcus sieus ditz am oli e entrometa aquels espertament e revolva am aquels aquo que es retengut.
It is necessary that the stretching is softened; and if any part of it is retained, the midwife should anoint some of her fingers with oil and gently insert them to loosen the retained part.

Donc si la partida del fet es fora-getada, lahoras les uncis sian permudatz entra loc le qual sia pus aut; e fay aysso entro que tot le fet sia fora-getat.
Then, if a part of the fetus is removed, the hooks should be moved to a higher place; and do this until the whole fetus is removed.

Mays si la ma es eyssida denant l’autra, e no es possible reduzir aquela per la coartacio de lu, lahoras cove que drap sia envolopat sobre aquella; e aprop extratz aquela entro que tota sia fora-getada, e inscideys aquela o en la junctura de la ma o en le coyde.
But if one hand comes out before the other, and it is not possible to reduce it due to its tightness, then cloth should be wrapped around it; and then extract it until it is completely removed, and cut it either at the wrist or the elbow.

E ayssi cove que fassas en l’autra ma e en les dos pes.
And you must do the same with the other hand and the two feet.

Mays si le cap del fet es gran, o accideys a lu coartacio en le eyssiment, o es en le cap de lu aygua ajustada, lahoras cove que entrometa entre les ditz espatum spinos e fenda le cap e extragua la aygua, o que discroba aquel am un instrument le qual es nompnat “alundat”, la forma del qual vindra am las formas dels autres instruments en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.
But if the fetus's head is large, or if it is constricted in the delivery, or if there is water in its head, then you must insert between the fingers a pointed spatula and pierce the head to extract the water, or use an instrument called “alundat,” whose shape will be described along with other instruments in the chapter near this one.

E semblantment fassa si·l fet es de gran cap per natura: e lahoras cove que inscida aquel am algematu, o que prengua aquel am alunda ayssi cum havem dit; e aprop extra les osses am les forceps.
And do similarly if the fetus has a naturally large head: then you must cut it with a knife, or take it with the alunda as we have mentioned; and then extract the bones with forceps.

E si le cap es eyssit e es coartat deves la furcula, lahoras sia fendut entro que la humiditat la qual es en le pietz sia efunduda.
And if the head has come out but is constricted at the clavicle, then it should be cut until the moisture in the chest is released.

Mays si no es complicat, ni obezeys a eyssiment, lahoras tu inscideys le cap tantost segon que a tu sira possible.
But if it is not complicated, nor responding to extraction, then you should cut the head as soon as possible as you are able.

E si le dejos del ventre es apostemat o es en lu ydropici, lahoras cove que tu perfores aquel entro que corro la humiditat que es en lu.
And if the lower abdomen is abscessed or has dropsy, then you must pierce it so that the moisture inside can flow out.

Mays si le fet es sobre les sieus pes, lahoras la atraccio de lu es leugiera e la direccio de lu a la boca de la mayre es leugiera.
But if the fetus is on its feet, then its traction is light and its direction to the mother's mouth is light.

Mays si es coartat deves le ventre e·l pietz, lahoras cove que tu extraguas aquel am drap le qual auras envolopat sobre la tua ma, e que fendes le ventre e·l pietz entro que corra aquo que es en aquels.
But if it is constricted around the belly and chest, then you must extract it with a cloth wrapped around your hand, and cut the belly and chest until what is inside flows out.

Mays si les autres membres so ostatz e torna le cap, lahoras la metrona entrometa la ma senestra; mays si la boca de la mayre es huberta, lahoras intrometa la ma en le preon de layre, e cerque am aquela le cap, e atira aquel am les ditz entro a la boca de la mayre, e aprop entrometa en lu un unci, o dos uncis, e atire lu am aquels.
But if the other limbs are out and the head remains, then the midwife should insert her left hand; but if the mother's mouth is open, then insert the hand into the throat, search for the head, and pull it with the fingers to the mother's mouth, then insert a hook, or two hooks, and pull it out with them.

E si la boca de la mayre es coartada per apostema caut le qual accideys a l’u, lahoras cove que no sia trebelhat sobre lu; abantz cove lahoras aministrar efusio de causas humidas grassas.
And if the mother's mouth is constricted by an abscess that occurred, then it must not be worked on; instead, moist and fatty remedies should be administered.

E aministre emplastres; e segua le pacient en ayguas que mollifican e humectan.
And apply plasters; and have the patient follow a regimen of baths that soften and moisten.

E si le fet es sobre le sieu costat, lahoras si possible es, sia agulat: e sia aministrat aquo que havem dit en le fet viu.
And if the fetus is on its side, then if possible, it should be turned: and follow what we have said for a live fetus.

E si aquo no es possible, lahoras sia inscidit en pessas, e sia extrayt.
And if this is not possible, then it should be cut into pieces and extracted.

E cove que non layssas alcuna causa dedintz de la segondina.
And it is necessary that no part of the placenta is left inside.

E cum tu auras complida tota la tua opperacio, lahoras aministra aquo que havem dit de la curacio en les apostemas cautz les quals accideysso de la mayre.
And when you have completed all your operations, then administer what we have said about treating the abscesses that occur in the mother.

E si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras deyssendas en ayguas stipticas e aministra l’autra curacio.
And if there is a flow of blood, then have her sit in astringent baths and administer other treatments.

E yeu ja e vist una femna en le ventre de la qual era fet mort, e aprop sobre aquel foc autra veguada emprenhada, e aprop foc mort es le fet autre.
And I have seen a woman in whose womb there was a dead fetus, and then she became pregnant again, and the fetus died again.

Accidit al u aprop lonc temps apostema en le sieu embelic; e inflat es entro que foc ubert, e comensec a getar brac.
It happened to her after a long time an abscess in her navel; and it swelled until it opened, and began to discharge pus.

E yeu fu appelhat a la cura de lu, e medicat a lu per lonc temps, e la plagua no es consolidada.
And I was called to treat it, and treated it for a long time, and the wound did not heal.

Adonc yeu pausegui sobre lu de alscunas causas emplastra de forta atraccio, e eyssic de lu un os, e aprop passero alcus jorns, e eyssic un autre os; e yeu fu trop meravilhat, cum en le ventre no sia os.
Then I applied to it some strong drawing plasters, and a bone came out, and after a few days, another bone came out; and I was greatly amazed, as there are no bones in the belly.

E adonc yeu cogitegui que eran dels osses del fet mort.
And then I thought that they were the bones of the dead fetus.

Donc yeu enguisigui la plagua, e extrayssi de lu motz osses , la femna existent en las sieuas milhos disposicios, e ja visquec en tal manieyra per lonc temps, correc de lu un petit de brac.
Then I treated the wound, and extracted many bones from it, with the woman being in better condition, and she lived in this way for a long time, discharging a little pus.

E yeu no afermegui asso esser stranh, sino quar en aquo es sciensa e ajutori ad aquo que le metge artifec am la ma per curacio aministra.
And I do not consider this strange, but rather see it as knowledge and help in what the skilled physician can administer by hand for healing.

De las formas dels instrumentz que so necessaris a extrayre le fet.
On the forms of the instruments necessary to extract the fetus.

Forma de vertitge am la qual es uberta la mayre:
Form of the screw with which the mother is opened:

Aquesta es la forma de strenhedor en le qual so engualhatz les libres, al qual engualhament sian dos virtitges en doas extremitatz de dos futz.
This is the form of the screw in which the books are joined, in which there are two screws at the ends of two rods.

May empero aquesta virtitge cove que sia pus subtil de strictori, e sia fayt o de eba o de fust de boys.
However, this screw must be more delicate in structure, and be made of ebony or boxwood.

E sia la latitut de quascun fust quays dos ditz e le marge de quascu amdos quays un dit, e la longitut de quascu es un palm e mig; e en le mieg loc de dos fustz so dos ajustaments de aquel meteys fustz les quals ja son fermatz, dels quals la longitut es la maytat de un palm e un pauc mes, e la latitut de quascu es quay dos ditz, o un pauc mes.
And the width of each rod should be about two fingers, and the edge of each about one finger, and the length of each is one and a half palms; and in the middle of the two rods are two joints of the same wood that are already fixed, whose length is half a palm and a little more, and the width of each is about two fingers, or a little more.

E aquestz dos additamentz sian entromeses en la boca de la mayre per que sia uberta am aquels quan tu revolves las doas prescriptas virtigges.
